I personally don't like the prison design where you have to click on a bed at some point to be imprisoned. It detracts from the narrative for me because no knowledgeable player would click on a bed inside of a prison unless it was for theater. There is no way to force another player to use the bed aside from commands, mods, or hacking. The only way to make the bed trap believable is if you convert it into a prison while they are gone, and then kill them. I would like to see a compact prison designed around something like that. Bonus points if you can incorporate a death trap into the base so that you do not have to locate the person, corner them, force them into pvp, and win. It is quite difficult to kill someone who has fireworks and rockets given the fact that they can fly above the build limit and log out, making themselves untouchable to traps and inconvenient to spawn camp.
